The following table was created as response to the SQL query
SELECT sbs_sbsnumber "SBS number", sbs_sbsname "SBS name", pgf_name "plant growth form", pgf_genname "gen. plant growth form", pgf_valid "record validity", ref_refname "reference", or_origrefname "original reference" FROM (SELECT r_pgf.pgf_name, sbs.sbs_sbsnumber, sbs.sbs_sbsname, r_pgf.pgf_genname, r_pgf.pgf_valid, r_pgf.ref_refname, r_pgf.or_origrefname, r_pgf.pgf_sbsnumber FROM (SELECT speciesno AS sbs_sbsnumber, fullname AS sbs_sbsname FROM (SELECT fullname, speciesno, familyname, isinledalist from (select fullname, speciesno, family as familyid, isinledalist from taxon where specieslist = 60028) natural join taxonomicfamily)) sbs JOIN (SELECT pgf_orf.pgf_sbsnumber, pgf_orf.pgf_name, pgf_orf.pgf_genname, pgf_orf.pgf_valid, r.ref_refname, pgf_orf.or_origrefname FROM (SELECT referenceid AS ref_referenceid, refname AS ref_refname FROM (select referenceid, refname, reftypeid from reference)) r LEFT JOIN (SELECT pgf.pgf_sbsnumber, pgf.pgf_name, pgf.pgf_genname, pgf.pgf_valid, pgf.pgf_referenceid, orf.or_origrefname FROM (SELECT sbsnumber AS pgf_sbsnumber, plantgrowthformname AS pgf_name, genplantgrowthformname AS pgf_genname, valid AS pgf_valid, referenceid AS pgf_referenceid, originalreference AS pgf_origreferenceid FROM (SELECT plantgrowthformid, created_when, updated_when, updatedwho, valid, validsince, validuntil, sbsnumber, taxonid, referenceid, originalreference, batchid, p_comment, plantgrowthformtypeid, genplantgrowthformtypeid, plantgrowthformname, genplantgrowthformname
FROM
	(SELECT plantgrowthformid, created_when, updated_when, updatedwho, valid, validsince, validuntil, taxonid, referenceid, originalreference, batchid, p_comment, a.plantgrowthformtypeid, a.plantgrowthformtypename AS plantgrowthformname, b.plantgrowthformtypename AS genplantgrowthformname, b.plantgrowthformtypeid AS genplantgrowthformtypeid
	FROM
		(SELECT * FROM PLANTGROWTHFORM NATURAL join PLANTGROWTHFORMTYPE_LV) a
		join
		PLANTGROWTHFORMTYPE_LV b
		ON a.plantgrowthformtypeid - MOD(a.plantgrowthformtypeid,100) = b.plantgrowthformtypeid
	)
	NATURAL join
	TAXONTOSBSASSIGNMENT WHERE valid IN (-2, 1))) pgf FULL JOIN (SELECT origreferenceid AS or_origrefid, origrefname AS or_origrefname FROM (select referenceid as origreferenceid, refname as origrefname, reftypeid as origreftypeid from reference)) orf ON pgf.pgf_origreferenceid = orf.or_origrefid) pgf_orf ON r.ref_referenceid = pgf_orf.pgf_referenceid) r_pgf ON sbs.sbs_sbsnumber = r_pgf.pgf_sbsnumber)
on Mon Apr 26 11:04:46 CEST 2010 .
